<p><strong>Features</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports basic (inline content) and viewport (shared viewport) patterns</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Hover and click trigger support with configurable delays</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Keyboard navigation with arrow keys, Tab, Home/End</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Animated indicator that follows the active trigger</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Smooth content animations with viewport positioning</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Horizontal and vertical orientation</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">RTL (right-to-left) support</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Dismissible with click outside or Escape key</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="anatomy" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Anatomy<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#anatomy"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Check the navigation menu anatomy and part names.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute to help identify them in the DOM.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="">No anatomy available for <!-- -->navigation-menu</div>
<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the navigation menu package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> navigationMenu</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/navigation-menu&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>The navigation menu package exports two key functions:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - State machine logic.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
</ul>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Pass a unique <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">useMachine</code> so generated element ids stay predictable.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Then use the framework integration helpers:</p>
<div data-scope="tabs" data-part="root" id="tabs:navigation-menu/usage.mdx" data-orientation="horizontal" dir="ltr" class="w_full max-w_768px bd-w_1px my_8 bg_bg.code.block bdr_6px"><div </span></div></pre><button type="button" class="px_2 py_1 gap_1 bd-w_1px pos_absolute right_5 top_3 d_flex ai_center fs_xs bg_bg.subtle bd-c_border.subtle cursor_pointer hover:bg_bg.muted"><svg stroke="currentColor" fill="none" stroke-width="2" viewBox="0 0 24 24" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="w_1em h_1em va_middle" height="1em" width="1em" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M8 5H6a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2v-1M8 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M8 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2m0 0h2a2 2 0 012 2v3m2 4H10m0 0l3-3m-3 3l3 3"></path></svg><span>Copy</span></button></div></div></div>
<p>The basic pattern places content directly within each item. This is suitable for
simple dropdown menus where each dropdown appears below its trigger.</p>
<h3 id="advanced-pattern-with-viewport" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Advanced pattern with viewport<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#advanced-pattern-with-viewport"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The viewport pattern uses a shared viewport container for all content. This
enables smooth transitions and better performance for complex navigation
layouts.</p>
<p>In this pattern:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Content is rendered inside a shared <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">viewport</code> element</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">The viewport automatically positions itself relative to the active trigger</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">You must include <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">triggerProxy</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">viewportProxy</code> for proper focus
management</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>When to use viewport pattern:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Complex navigation with varying content sizes</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Smooth animated transitions between different content</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Header navigation bars (like on e-commerce sites)</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">When you want a single shared container for all dropdowns</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="controlling-the-navigation-menu" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlling the navigation menu<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlling-the-navigation-menu"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To control which item is currently open, pass the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code>
properties to the machine.</p>

data-framework="react"><pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line highlight-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span <h3 id="setting-initial-open-item" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting initial open item<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-initial-open-item"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultValue</code> to start with a specific item open.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>navigationMenu<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="listening-for-value-changes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for value changes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-value-changes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the open item changes, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code> callback is invoked with the new
value.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>navigationMenu<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;nav&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function">onValueChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { value: string }</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;Current open item:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">value</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="adding-an-animated-indicator" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Adding an animated indicator<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#adding-an-animated-indicator"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>

</span></span><span class="code-line highlight-line"><span class="token plain-text">    </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span><span class="token method function property-access">api</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getIndicatorProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">

</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">  </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>div</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text"></span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>nav</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span></div></pre><button type="button" class="px_2 py_1 gap_1 bd-w_1px pos_absolute right_5 top_3 d_flex ai_center fs_xs bg_bg.subtle bd-c_border.subtle cursor_pointer hover:bg_bg.muted"><svg stroke="currentColor" fill="none" stroke-width="2" viewBox="0 0 24 24" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="w_1em h_1em va_middle" height="1em" width="1em" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M8 5H6a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2v-1M8 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M8 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2m0 0h2a2 2 0 012 2v3m2 4H10m0 0l3-3m-3 3l3 3"></path></svg><span>Copy</span></button></div></div><div data-scope="tabs" data-part="content" dir="ltr" id="tabs:navigation-menu/with-indicator.mdx:content-vue" tabindex="0" aria-labelledby="tabs:navigation-menu/with-indicator.mdx:trigger-vue" role="tabpanel" data-ownedby="tabs:navigation-menu/with-indicator.mdx:list" data-orientation="horizontal" hidden="" class="pos_relative mt_-6 focusVisible:ring_2px_solid_blue"><div class="prose" id="snippet" data-framework="vue"><pre class="prose language-html"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>nav</span> <span class="token attr-name">v-bind</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span>api.getRootProps()<span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>

</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token comment">&lt;!-- ... items ... --&gt;</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token attr-name">v-bind</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span>api.getIndicatorProps()<span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>

<p>The indicator automatically transitions to match the active trigger&#x27;s position
and size using CSS variables.</p>
<h3 id="configuring-hover-delays" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Configuring hover delays<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#configuring-hover-delays"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>You can customize the delay before opening and closing on hover:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>navigationMenu<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">openDelay</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">300</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token comment">// Delay before opening on hover (default: 200ms)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">closeDelay</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">400</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token comment">// Delay before closing on pointer leave (default: 300ms)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p><strong>Tip</strong>: Longer delays provide a more forgiving user experience but can feel
less responsive.</p>
<h3 id="disabling-hover-or-click-triggers" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disabling hover or click triggers<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disabling-hover-or-click-triggers"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>You can disable hover or click triggers independently:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>navigationMenu<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">disableHoverTrigger</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token comment">// Only open on click</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token comment">// OR</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">disableClickTrigger</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token comment">// Only open on hover</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token comment">// OR</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">disablePointerLeaveClose</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token comment">// Prevents closing when pointer leaves</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disableHoverTrigger</code> — Prevents opening on hover (click only)</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disableClickTrigger</code> — Prevents opening on click (hover only)</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disablePointerLeaveClose</code> — Prevents closing when pointer leaves</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="changing-orientation" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Changing orientation<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#changing-orientation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The default orientation is horizontal. To create a vertical navigation menu:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>navigationMenu<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">orientation</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;vertical&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>This affects keyboard navigation (arrow keys) and indicator positioning.</p>
<h3 id="disabling-items" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disabling items<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disabling-items"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To disable a navigation item, pass <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disabled: true</code> to the item props:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getItemProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">value</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;products&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">disabled</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">  </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>button</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getTriggerProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">value</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;products&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">disabled</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">    Products
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">  </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>button</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text"></span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>div</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>Disabled items cannot be opened and are skipped during keyboard navigation.</p>
<h3 id="indicating-current-page" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Indicating current page<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#indicating-current-page"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To highlight the current page link, use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">current</code> prop:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>a</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getLinkProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">value</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;products&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">current</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">Products</span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>a</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>This adds <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-current</code> attribute and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">aria-current=&quot;page&quot;</code> for accessibility.</p>
<h3 id="controlling-link-close-behavior" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlling link close behavior<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlling-link-close-behavior"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeOnClick</code> in <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getLinkProps</code> to keep content open after link click.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>a</span>
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag">  <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getLinkProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token spread">    <span class="token literal-property property">value</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;products&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token spread">    <span class="token literal-property property">closeOnClick</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token spread">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span>
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">  Products
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text"></span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>a</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="aligning-the-shared-viewport" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Aligning the shared viewport<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#aligning-the-shared-viewport"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When using the viewport pattern, set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">align</code> on <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getViewportProps</code> or
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getViewportPositionerProps</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span>
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag">  <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getViewportProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token spread">    <span class="token literal-property property">align</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;start&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token spread">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span>
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="rtl-support" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">RTL support<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#rtl-support"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The navigation menu supports right-to-left languages. Set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dir</code> property to
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">rtl</code>:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>navigationMenu<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">dir</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;rtl&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute you can target in CSS.</p>
<h3 id="open-and-closed-states" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Open and closed states<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#open-and-closed-states"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When content is open or closed, it receives a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-state</code> attribute:</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;content&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;open|closed&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* Styles for open or closed content */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;open|closed&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* Styles for open or closed trigger */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;viewport&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;open|closed&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* Styles for viewport open/closed state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="selected-item-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Selected item state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#selected-item-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When an item is selected (open), it receives <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-state=&quot;open&quot;</code>:</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;open&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* Styles for open item */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="disabled-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disabled state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disabled-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Disabled items have a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-disabled</code> attribute:</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* Styles for disabled items */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* Styles for disabled triggers */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="orientation-styles" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Orientation styles<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#orientation-styles"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>All parts have a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-orientation</code> attribute:</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-orientation</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;horizontal|vertical&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* Orientation-specific styles */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;list&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-orientation</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;horizontal&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;list&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-orientation</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;vertical&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">flex-direction</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> column<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="current-link-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Current link state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#current-link-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Links marked as current have a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-current</code> attribute:</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;link&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-current</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* Styles for current page link */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="styling-the-indicator" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Styling the indicator<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-the-indicator"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The indicator uses CSS variables for positioning and sizing:</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;indicator&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line">    width <span class="token number">250</span><span class="token unit">ms</span> ease<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    height <span class="token number">250</span><span class="token unit">ms</span> ease<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;indicator&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-orientation</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;horizontal&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;indicator&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-orientation</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;vertical&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

<h3 id="styling-the-viewport" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Styling the viewport<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-the-viewport"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The viewport uses CSS variables for positioning and sizing:</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;viewport&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">position</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> absolute<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">width</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token function">var</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token variable">--viewport-width</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">height</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token function">var</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token variable">--viewport-height</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">transition</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    width <span class="token number">300</span><span class="token unit">ms</span> ease<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    height <span class="token number">300</span><span class="token unit">ms</span> ease<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="arrow-styling" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Arrow styling<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#arrow-styling"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The arrow can be styled using CSS variables:</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token variable">--arrow-size</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token number">20</span><span class="token unit">px</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;arrow&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">width</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token function">var</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token variable">--arrow-size</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">height</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token function">var</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token variable">--arrow-size</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">background</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token color">white</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">rotate</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token number">45</span><span class="token unit">deg</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="motion-attributes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Motion attributes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#motion-attributes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When using the viewport pattern, content elements receive <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-motion</code>
attributes for directional animations:</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;content&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-motion</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;from-start&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">animation</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> slideFromStart <span class="token number">250</span><span class="token unit">ms</span> ease<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;content&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-motion</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;from-end&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">animation</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> slideFromEnd <span class="token number">250</span><span class="token unit">ms</span> ease<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;content&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-motion</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;to-start&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">animation</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> slideToStart <span class="token number">250</span><span class="token unit">ms</span> ease<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;content&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-motion</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;to-end&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">animation</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> slideToEnd <span class="token number">250</span><span class="token unit">ms</span> ease<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p><strong>Tip</strong>: The motion direction indicates where the content is coming from
(from-start/from-end) or going to (to-start/to-end), enabling context-aware
animations when switching between items.</p>
<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The navigation menu machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ root: string; list: string; item: string; trigger: (value: string) =&gt; string; content: (value: string) =&gt; string; viewport: string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the elements in the machine.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The controlled value of the navigation menu</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The default value of the navigation menu.

<h3 id="machine-api" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine API<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-api"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The navigation menu <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods:</p>

<h3 id="keyboard-interactions" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Keyboard Interactions<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#keyboard-interactions"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_8px pl_0! li-t_none li-pos_inside dvd-y_1px"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">ArrowDown</kbd></div><div>When focus is on trigger (vertical orientation), moves focus to the next trigger.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">ArrowUp</kbd></div><div>When focus is on trigger (vertical orientation), moves focus to the previous trigger.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">ArrowRight</kbd></div><div><span>When focus is on trigger (horizontal orientation), moves focus to the next trigger.<br />When focus is on content, moves focus to the next link.</span></div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column navigation menu displays links with optional dropdown content.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cresources pkg=\"@zag-js/navigation-menu\"\u003e\n\u003cshowcase id=\"NavigationMenu\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFeatures\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports basic (inline content) and viewport (shared viewport) patterns\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eHover and click trigger support with configurable delays\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eKeyboard navigation with arrow keys, Tab, Home/End\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAnimated indicator that follows the active trigger\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSmooth content animations with viewport positioning\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eHorizontal and vertical orientation\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eRTL (right-to-left) support\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eDismissible with click outside or Escape key\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eInstallation\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eInstall the navigation menu package:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"navigation-menu/installation.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eAnatomy\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eCheck the navigation menu anatomy and part names.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eEach part includes a \u003ccode\u003edata-part\u003c/code\u003e attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003canatomy id=\"navigation-menu\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eUsage\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eImport the navigation menu package:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003eimport * as navigationMenu from \"@zag-js/navigation-menu\"\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe navigation menu package exports two key functions:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003emachine\u003c/code\u003e - State machine logic.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003econnect\u003c/code\u003e - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003ePass a unique \u003ccode\u003eid\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003euseMachine\u003c/code\u003e so generated element ids stay predictable.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThen use the framework integration helpers:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"navigation-menu/usage.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe basic pattern places content directly within each item. This is suitable for\nsimple dropdown menus where each dropdown appears below its trigger.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eAdvanced pattern with viewport\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe viewport pattern uses a shared viewport container for all content. This\nenables smooth transitions and better performance for complex navigation\nlayouts.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eIn this pattern:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eContent is rendered inside a shared \u003ccode\u003eviewport\u003c/code\u003e element\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eThe viewport automatically positions itself relative to the active trigger\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eYou must include \u003ccode\u003etriggerProxy\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eviewportProxy\u003c/code\u003e for proper focus\nmanagement\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"navigation-menu/viewport-usage.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWhen to use viewport pattern:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eComplex navigation with varying content sizes\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSmooth animated transitions between different content\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eHeader navigation bars (like on e-commerce sites)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eWhen you want a single shared container for all dropdowns\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eControlling the navigation menu\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo control which item is currently open, pass the \u003ccode\u003evalue\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eonValueChange\u003c/code\u003e\nproperties to the machine.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"navigation-menu/controlled.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSetting initial open item\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003edefaultValue\u003c/code\u003e to start with a specific item open.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(navigationMenu.machine, {\n  defaultValue: \"products\",\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eListening for value changes\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen the open item changes, the \u003ccode\u003eonValueChange\u003c/code\u003e callback is invoked with the new\nvalue.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{3-6}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(navigationMenu.machine, {\n  id: \"nav\",\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string }\n    console.log(\"Current open item:\", details.value)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eAdding an animated indicator\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo show a visual indicator that animates to the active trigger, render the\nindicator within the list container:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"navigation-menu/with-indicator.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe indicator automatically transitions to match the active trigger's position\nand size using CSS variables.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eConfiguring hover delays\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eYou can customize the delay before opening and closing on hover:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2-3}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(navigationMenu.machine, {\n  openDelay: 300, // Delay before opening on hover (default: 200ms)\n  closeDelay: 400, // Delay before closing on pointer leave (default: 300ms)\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTip\u003c/strong\u003e: Longer delays provide a more forgiving user experience but can feel\nless responsive.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eDisabling hover or click triggers\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eYou can disable hover or click triggers independently:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2-6}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(navigationMenu.machine, {\n  disableHoverTrigger: true, // Only open on click\n  // OR\n  disableClickTrigger: true, // Only open on hover\n  // OR\n  disablePointerLeaveClose: true, // Prevents closing when pointer leaves\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003edisableHoverTrigger\u003c/code\u003e — Prevents opening on hover (click only)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003edisableClickTrigger\u003c/code\u003e — Prevents opening on click (hover only)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003edisablePointerLeaveClose\u003c/code\u003e — Prevents closing when pointer leaves\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eChanging orientation\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe default orientation is horizontal. likely forgot to import, pass, or provide it.\")}"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"12:T247d,"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"A navigation menu displays links with optional dropdown content.\n\n\u003cResources pkg=\"@zag-js/navigation-menu\" /\u003e\n\n\u003cShowcase id=\"NavigationMenu\" /\u003e\n\n**Features**\n\n- Supports basic (inline content) and viewport (shared viewport) patterns\n- Hover and click trigger support with configurable delays\n- Keyboard navigation with arrow keys, Tab, Home/End\n- Animated indicator that follows the active trigger\n- Smooth content animations with viewport positioning\n- Horizontal and vertical orientation\n- RTL (right-to-left) support\n- Dismissible with click outside or Escape key\n\n## Installation\n\nInstall the navigation menu package:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"navigation-menu/installation.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\nCheck the navigation menu anatomy and part names.\n\n\u003e Each part includes a `data-part` attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"navigation-menu\" /\u003e\n\n## Usage\n\nImport the navigation menu package:\n\n```jsx\nimport * as navigationMenu from \"@zag-js/navigation-menu\"\n```\n\nThe navigation menu package exports two key functions:\n\n- `machine` - State machine logic.\n- `connect` - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\n\n\u003e Pass a unique `id` to `useMachine` so generated element ids stay predictable.\n\nThen use the framework integration helpers:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"navigation-menu/usage.mdx\" /\u003e\n\nThe basic pattern places content directly within each item. This is suitable for\nsimple dropdown menus where each dropdown appears below its trigger.\n\n### Advanced pattern with viewport\n\nThe viewport pattern uses a shared viewport container for all content. This\nenables smooth transitions and better performance for complex navigation\nlayouts.\n\nIn this pattern:\n\n- Content is rendered inside a shared `viewport` element\n- The viewport automatically positions itself relative to the active trigger\n- You must include `triggerProxy` and `viewportProxy` for proper focus\n  management\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"navigation-menu/viewport-usage.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n**When to use viewport pattern:**\n\n- Complex navigation with varying content sizes\n- Smooth animated transitions between different content\n- Header navigation bars (like on e-commerce sites)\n- When you want a single shared container for all dropdowns\n\n### Controlling the navigation menu\n\nTo control which item is currently open, pass the `value` and `onValueChange`\nproperties to the machine.\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"navigation-menu/controlled.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Setting initial open item\n\nUse `defaultValue` to start with a specific item open.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(navigationMenu.machine, {\n  defaultValue: \"products\",\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for value changes\n\nWhen the open item changes, the `onValueChange` callback is invoked with the new\nvalue.\n\n```jsx {3-6}\nconst service = useMachine(navigationMenu.machine, {\n  id: \"nav\",\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string }\n    console.log(\"Current open item:\", details.value)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Adding an animated indicator\n\nTo show a visual indicator that animates to the active trigger, render the\nindicator within the list container:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"navigation-menu/with-indicator.mdx\" /\u003e\n\nThe indicator automatically transitions to match the active trigger's position\nand size using CSS variables.\n\n### Configuring hover delays\n\nYou can customize the delay before opening and closing on hover:\n\n```jsx {2-3}\nconst service = useMachine(navigationMenu.machine, {\n  openDelay: 300, // Delay before opening on hover (default: 200ms)\n  closeDelay: 400, // Delay before closing on pointer leave (default: 300ms)\n})\n```\n\n**Tip**: Longer delays provide a more forgiving user experience but can feel\nless responsive.\n\n### Disabling hover or click triggers\n\nYou can disable hover or click triggers independently:\n\n```jsx {2-6}\nconst service = useMachine(navigationMenu.machine, {\n  disableHoverTrigger: true, // Only open on click\n  // OR\n  disableClickTrigger: true, // Only open on hover\n  // OR\n  disablePointerLeaveClose: true, // Prevents closing when pointer leaves\n})\n```\n\n- `disableHoverTrigger` — Prevents opening on hover (click only)\n- `disableClickTrigger` — Prevents opening on click (hover only)\n- `disablePointerLeaveClose` — Prevents closing when pointer leaves\n\n### Changing orientation\n\nThe default orientation is horizontal. To create a vertical navigation menu:\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(navigationMenu.machine, {\n  orientation: \"vertical\",\n})\n```\n\nThis affects keyboard navigation (arrow keys) and indicator positioning.\n\n### Disabling items\n\nTo disable a navigation item, pass `disabled: true` to the item props:\n\n```jsx\n\u003cdiv {...api.getItemProps({ value: \"products\", disabled: true })}\u003e\n  \u003cbutton {...api.getTriggerProps({ value: \"products\", disabled: true })}\u003e\n    Products\n  \u003c/button\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n```\n\nDisabled items cannot be opened and are skipped during keyboard navigation.\n\n### Indicating current page\n\nTo highlight the current page link, use the `current` prop:\n\n```jsx\n\u003ca {...api.getLinkProps({ value: \"products\", current: true })}\u003eProducts\u003c/a\u003e\n```\n\nThis adds `data-current` attribute and `aria-current=\"page\"` for accessibility.\n\n### Controlling link close behavior\n\nUse `closeOnClick` in `getLinkProps` to keep content open after link click.\n\n```jsx\n\u003ca\n  {...api.getLinkProps({\n    value: \"products\",\n    closeOnClick: false,\n  })}\n\u003e\n  Products\n\u003c/a\u003e\n```\n\n### Aligning the shared viewport\n\nWhen using the viewport pattern, set `align` on `getViewportProps` or\n`getViewportPositionerProps`.\n\n```jsx\n\u003cdiv\n  {...api.getViewportProps({\n    align: \"start\",\n  })}\n/\u003e\n```\n\n### RTL support\n\nThe navigation menu supports right-to-left languages. Set the `dir` property to\n`rtl`:\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(navigationMenu.machine, {\n  dir: \"rtl\",\n})\n```\n\n## Styling guide\n\nEach part includes a `data-part` attribute you can target in CSS.\n\n### Open and closed states\n\nWhen content is open or closed, it receives a `data-state` attribute:\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"content\"][data-state=\"open|closed\"] {\n  /* Styles for open or closed content */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"trigger\"][data-state=\"open|closed\"] {\n  /* Styles for open or closed trigger */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"viewport\"][data-state=\"open|closed\"] {\n  /* Styles for viewport open/closed state */\n}\n```\n\n### Selected item state\n\nWhen an item is selected (open), it receives `data-state=\"open\"`:\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"item\"][data-state=\"open\"] {\n  /* Styles for open item */\n}\n```\n\n### Disabled state\n\nDisabled items have a `data-disabled` attribute:\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"item\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* Styles for disabled items */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"trigger\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* Styles for disabled triggers */\n}\n```\n\n### Orientation styles\n\nAll parts have a `data-orientation` attribute:\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"root\"][data-orientation=\"horizontal|vertical\"] {\n  /* Orientation-specific styles */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"list\"][data-orientation=\"horizontal\"] {\n  display: flex;\n  flex-direction: row;\n}\n\n[data-part=\"list\"][data-orientation=\"vertical\"] {\n  display: flex;\n  flex-direction: column;\n}\n```\n\n### Current link state\n\nLinks marked as current have a `data-current` attribute:\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"link\"][data-current] {\n  /* Styles for current page link */\n}\n```\n\n### Styling the indicator\n\nThe indicator uses CSS variables for positioning and sizing:\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"indicator\"] {\n  position: absolute;\n  transition:\n    translate 250ms ease,\n    width 250ms ease,\n    height 250ms ease;\n}\n\n[data-part=\"indicator\"][data-orientation=\"horizontal\"] {\n  left: 0;\n  translate: var(--trigger-x) 0;\n  width: var(--trigger-width);\n}\n\n[data-part=\"indicator\"][data-orientation=\"vertical\"] {\n  top: 0;\n  translate: 0 var(--trigger-y);\n  height: var(--trigger-height);\n}\n```\n\n### Styling the viewport\n\nThe viewport uses CSS variables for positioning and sizing:\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"viewport\"] {\n  position: absolute;\n  width: var(--viewport-width);\n  height: var(--viewport-height);\n  transition:\n    width 300ms ease,\n    height 300ms ease;\n}\n```\n\n### Arrow styling\n\nThe arrow can be styled using CSS variables:\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"root\"] {\n  --arrow-size: 20px;\n}\n\n[data-part=\"arrow\"] {\n  width: var(--arrow-size);\n  height: var(--arrow-size);\n  background: white;\n  rotate: 45deg;\n}\n```\n\n### Motion attributes\n\nWhen using the viewport pattern, content elements receive `data-motion`\nattributes for directional animations:\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"content\"][data-motion=\"from-start\"] {\n  animation: slideFromStart 250ms ease;\n}\n\n[data-part=\"content\"][data-motion=\"from-end\"] {\n  animation: slideFromEnd 250ms ease;\n}\n\n[data-part=\"content\"][data-motion=\"to-start\"] {\n  animation: slideToStart 250ms ease;\n}\n\n[data-part=\"content\"][data-motion=\"to-end\"] {\n  animation: slideToEnd 250ms ease;\n}\n```\n\n**Tip**: The motion direction indicates where the content is coming from\n(from-start/from-end) or going to (to-start/to-end), enabling context-aware\nanimations when switching between items.\n\n## Methods and Properties\n\n### Machine Context\n\nThe navigation menu machine exposes the following context properties:\n\n\u003cContextTable name=\"navigation-menu\" /\u003e\n\n### Machine API\n\nThe navigation menu `api` exposes the following methods:\n\n\u003cApiTable name=\"navigation-menu\" /\u003e\n\n### Data Attributes\n\n\u003cDataAttrTable name=\"navigation-menu\" /\u003e\n\n### CSS Variables\n\n\u003cCssVarTable name=\"navigation-menu\" /\u003e\n\n## Accessibility\n\n### Keyboard Interactions\n\n\u003cKeyboardTable name=\"navigation-menu\" /\u003e"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"5:[\"$\",\"$Le\",null,{\"doc\":{\"title\":\"Navigation Menu\",\"description\":\"Using the navigation menu machine in your
